normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">仝瑞卿：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北大名县法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1945</span>年生，原是河北邯郸市劳动局（邯郸市社会保障中心）的干部，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年修炼法轮功后。中共迫害法轮功后，仝瑞卿遭到严重迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被劳教两年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年遭抓捕后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。因坚持修炼法轮功，他的儿媳、女婿、妹妹、妹夫遭劳教，姐姐含冤离世，妹妹被判刑，家族中有十余人遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，仝瑞卿被抓捕，后被关押在大名县万堤看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，大名县法院对仝瑞卿判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，仝瑞卿已被关押到河北唐山冀东监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/5/20/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E5%A4%A7%E5%90%8D%E5%8E%BF78%E5%B2%81%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%9D%E7%91%9E%E5%8D%BF%E3%80%81%E9%82%A2%E6%99%AF%E7%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-461056.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/5/20/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E5%A4%A7%E5%90%8D%E5%8E%BF78%E5%B2%81%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%9D%E7%91%9E%E5%8D%BF%E3%80%81%E9%82%A2%E6%99%AF%E7%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-461056.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">图丹（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因手持达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，并呼喊着口号独自游街示威，遂立即被警察拘捕。下落不明。现音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">图丹罗珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">藏族，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州（简称甘孜州）石渠县蒙宜乡蒙宜村人，原石渠县一中学教师，藏语言及文化倡导者，知名藏人学者和异见作家，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于中国一所大学，毕业后返回老家石渠县，并在当地的一所中学任教多年；曾因多次针对东西方文学、西藏文学和经济等领域发表藏文及汉文文章，深受读者好评，遂逐渐成为一名受境内学术界认可的藏人作家；然而因其发表反对（或不赞同）中共政府对藏人的同化政策文章，尽管其内容并未违宪，但却触碰到中共当局的敏感神经，以致于甘孜州当局指派石渠县警方多次对其进行警告，并肆意搜查其个人计算机等物品；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其被甘孜州石渠县警方莫名强行带走，自此杳无音讯；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其亲人才被当局告知，其已于同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被四川省甘孜藏族自治州石渠县法院以“分裂国家罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前疑似被羁押于甘孜藏族自治州石渠县看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/46.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">涂爱莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府法轮功学员。涂爱莲是孝南区新铺镇远大小学退休教师，退休才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，在家帮忙带孙女。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。涂爱莲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">拖合塔尔汗•拖列吾汗（哈萨克族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆建设兵团底<span lang="EN-US">6</span>师<span lang="EN-US">110</span>团<span lang="EN-US">2</span>连（民族连）职工，因集资兴建了一座清真寺，遂被新疆地方当局拘留，先是被送到当地的“去极端化教育中心”关押和洗脑教育，后又此处直接被拘捕抓走，至今毫无因信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">V</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">W.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万长春、万春琴、万红霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; minor-fareast;">万长春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省蚌埠市活石归正教会牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中旬，万长春牧师在云南丽江被警方抓捕，随后被押回安徽蚌埠，被以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑事拘留，羁押于蚌埠市看守所。万长春牧师所在的蚌埠市活石归正教会长老、执事同工都被不同程度的问话。教会财务全部被查，账户被冻结。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日万长春牧师家被警方抄家。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万春琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，蚌埠活石归正教会的牧师万长春被安徽省蚌埠市公安局禹会分局以“涉嫌非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑事拘留。随后，薛少强长老、万春琴同工，还有另外一个基督徒也以相同的罪名先后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又被更改罪名，蚌埠经禹会区人民检察院批准，蚌埠禹会分局以“诈骗罪”对他们批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/4.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/4.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">万红霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教一家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，随遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被闯入教学点的芜湖市戈江区警方将包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名老师莫名抓走，同时，教学点遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人被视为同案嫌疑人统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被准予取保候审外，万红霞及王明海等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被芜湖市戈江区检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕；据悉，其案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万筱萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南昌市西湖区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，万筱萍、杨金凤在永正外街，陈丽萍在站前西路锦峰大酒店门口被东湖公安分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，南昌市西湖区法院送达了对陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤及万金莲的刑事判决书，陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，万金莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。因<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均办理了「取保候审」，刑期均从判决执行之日起算。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万正平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省开江县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">，退休工人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，达州市开江县法轮功学员万正平被当地警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，以取保候审方式放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，万正平被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，开江县国保大队副大队长李翔将万正平抓捕到达州市看守所关押。后获悉其被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被转入四川省成都女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/9/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E7%9C%81%E5%BC%80%E6%B1%9F%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%87%E6%AD%A3%E5%B9%B3%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-434551.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/9/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E7%9C%81%E5%BC%80%E6%B1%9F%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%87%E6%AD%A3%E5%B9%B3%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-434551.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王爱弟</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河北唐山法轮功学员。家住唐山市丰润区白官屯镇田富庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，王爱弟被唐山市丰润区白官屯镇派出所人员抓捕、抄家，被抄走大量私人物品。时隔一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，王爱弟被遵化法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三千元。现今王爱弟被关押在何处，家属无法知晓。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王爱忠：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，祖籍中国浙江省金华市，现居住在广州，广东著名民主人士，南方街头运动倡导者之一。王爱忠因长期致力于推动南方街头运动，受到广东警方高度关注。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，六四<span lang="EN-US">25</span>周年前夕，王爱忠被广州警方于家中采取强制措施，随后以「涉嫌寻衅滋事罪」刑事拘留，关押在广州天河看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日取保候审释放。王爱忠是近年来一直坚持发声的民主人士，其在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>上的言论一直被中共当局密切监控。此次被抓捕，很可能是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日中午有人打电话给王爱忠，称其车被刮，诱其下楼，将人带走。随后，九名警察到王爱忠家搜查，向王妻出示了搜查证，搜走<span lang="EN-US">29</span>本书，两台电脑，一部手机。随后，还将王妻传唤到派出所，询问王爱忠的交往及言论情况，并警告勿发声。王爱忠随后遭刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，关押在广州天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉王爱忠案已经移送法院，等待开庭。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王爱忠案原定<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州不公开审理被取消 法院无任何理由和解释。王爱忠案于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日 上午<span lang="EN-US">9:30</span>分在广州天河区法院正式庭审，当庭宣判，王爱忠被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/05/blog-post_99.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/05/blog-post_99.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被当地<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及警察抓捕抄家，关押在江门看守所。看守所期间，王斌被强迫检查身体，警察用几十斤重的一字形八十公分铁锁把他的双脚分开八十公分，强迫他带着锁上楼梯，致使他双脚流血，身体遭受严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月后，日前，家属收到律师发来的江门市蓬江区法院《刑事判决书》，法院竟以王斌用<span lang="EN-US">VIVO</span>牌和中兴牌手机注册微信号建群传播真实消息为由，将他重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年并罚款人民币三万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王炳程：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北石家庄市法轮功学员。石家庄市长安区人。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日王炳程与其母亲刘朋被居住地派出所和长安公安分局抓捕，母女后被转入石家庄市第二看守所关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，桥西区法院对其母女二人均判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/26_4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/26_4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/4/%E7%9F%B3%E5%AE%B6%E5%BA%84%E5%B8%82%E5%88%98%E6%9C%8B%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E7%82%B3%E7%A8%8B%E6%AF%8D%E5%A5%B3%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-466759.html"><b lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王炳章：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1947</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河北省石家庄市籍人，基督徒，美国永久居民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年曾在美国创办《中国之春》杂志，被捕前任中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被不明身份的人在越南绑架后带到中国境内被警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日以“间谍和组织领导恐怖组织罪”被判无期徒刑。据其家人称，王炳章的身体现在随时有生命危险，狱方已在囚室安放了警报器，要求其一旦感到有任何不适马上按响警报；其深知自己健康状况频危，已经写好遗嘱，希望“请加拿大牧师前往中国为他送葬，并要求做遗体解剖公布死因”。目前在广东省韶关北江监狱（广东省韶关市浈江区梨市镇<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号信箱<span lang="EN-US">6-9</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">512140</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王彩云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，女，现年已年过七旬，原抚顺市龙凤矿职工。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在中共发动对法轮功修炼者的残酷迫害后，王彩云多次被非法关押、二次遭劳教迫害，曾遭惨无人道的酷刑摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，王彩云在东洲赶集又被抓捕。后抚顺市东洲区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在抚顺市看守所（南沟）对王彩云老太太开庭，法官说此案件不公开审理，没有让家属等人旁听，随后王彩云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金一万六千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/4_4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/4_4.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/2/%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E4%B8%9C%E6%B4%B2%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E6%9E%89%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A9%E4%BA%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-466688.html"><b mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省威海市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，王策与法轮功学员焦桂春在文登市葛家镇集市讲法轮功时，遭人恶告，被文登市公安局国保大队抓捕，随后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，文登市公安局国保警察闯到王策家将王策抓捕走。王策被荣成市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">安徽省阜阳市临泉县法轮功学员。王翠兰、王翠萍、王兰英、李海涛等人，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被临泉县法院秘密开庭、判刑和经济罚款。王翠兰遭临泉县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日送往安徽省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/12/451806.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王翠英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东菏泽市牡丹区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，原中共菏泽市委党校干部，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年退休。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年度，被评为“全省系统先进工作者”，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年度评为“全市系统先进工作者”，并全票通过副处级干部提拔。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日傍晚，王翠英在路边发送法轮功册子时，被跟踪监控的牡丹区公安局警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，王翠英被带入法庭，庭审期间，手铐、脚镣一直没有给卸掉。王翠英现在仍被非法关押在菏泽市看守所<span lang="EN-US">.2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉王翠英已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款两万元。家人去找审判长范虹要判决书不给，判决书内容、文号一律不给说，整个过程支支吾吾、闪烁其词，反复询问才得知其实三月十八日已经下达判决书，并说王翠英已提出上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王德振：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省廊坊市广阳区九州岛镇刘官营村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，王德振去固安县知子营集宣传法轮功，被固安城东派出所人员抓捕，当日人被放回，汽车被扣下。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，王德振去要车，被固安城东派出所警察构陷，并刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，王德振被视频开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。王德振提出上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457131.html#23224211054-10"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王东吉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王东霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南平顶山法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，原中平煤公司一矿职工，家住河南省平顶山市卫东区。王东霞于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被平顶山湛河区轻工路派出所警察抓捕、抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.minghui.tv/mh/articles/2022/11/23/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%B9%B3%E9%A1%B6%E5%B1%B1%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E4%B8%9C%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-452271.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://www.minghui.tv/mh/articles/2022/11/23/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%B9%B3%E9%A1%B6%E5%B1%B1%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E4%B8%9C%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-452271.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王恩英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，辽宁朝阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年王恩英曾因为发法轮功资料被抓捕。在被关押期间，她绝食反迫害，遭到警察野蛮灌食折磨。王恩英后被中共当地法院判刑三年，被关押到辽宁女子监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午，朝阳市法轮功学员王恩英、张玉凤、张秀英在朝阳市凌北乡集市上发法轮功资料，被便衣警察抓捕到高铁派出所。之后，锦州铁路公安处、朝阳市北塔公安分局警察联合对三名法轮功学员抄家。她们随后被关押在锦州市女子看守所。近日，王恩英、张玉凤、张秀英、三名朝阳市法轮功学员被判刑。张玉凤和张秀英分别被锦州凌海法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，王恩英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。王恩英的刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/1_12.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/1_12.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王凤芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王甘霖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阆中市人，江苏省南京市常住居民，原多家媒体记者及相关负责人；原“磅礴新闻”总编辑，著名调查记者，资深媒体人，坊间誉为“中国实力派调查记者”，异见媒体人，中国在押政治犯。早年大学阶段，曾通过自学考试攻读大学本科法律专业；毕业后进入新闻媒体行业，并逐渐成为多家媒体知名调查记者和媒体负责人；曾因在业界以擅长调查性报导和涉法报导着称，而被安徽卫视《记者档案》栏目在<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日以“调查记者王甘霖”为题进行专题报导，并从此人称“中国实力派调查记者”；但因其秉性率真耿直，故在媒体圈内颇有争议，并曾与另一媒体人因理念不合而公开对撕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因将国内<span lang="EN-US">6</span>家媒体和网站（后又追加百度、新浪网）先后告上南京市江宁区法院和南京市中级法院，故而引发社会广议；又因其刊发过不少轰动性调查报导，并且因此而推动过不少案件进展，遂得罪许多相关人士；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-17</span>日，其突然失踪，后得知因一篇监督报导而引发牢狱之灾，被江苏省邳州市警方莫名跨境抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日（或更长时日），被连续两次指定居所监视居住（实为秘押）；秘押期间，曾惨遭酷刑虐待；曾被坐老虎凳<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，即第一次监视居住期间，被连续坐老虎凳<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天，第二次监视居住期间，被连续坐老虎凳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天；曾被持续<span lang="EN-US">36</span>个小时不让吃任何食物，以致因患有严重糖尿病而使其身体变得极度虚弱；后又被江邳州市警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转为拘捕，指控其因与另一位张姓媒体人“自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年以来，使用‘獬法’和‘等辩’等系列自媒体账号，以营利为目的，对鲁、晋、贵、粤等省的重大刑事案件及党委政府进行负面炒作，从事有偿发贴、散步虚假信息和有偿删帖等”，所以其言行已构成“非法经营罪”，应予以逮捕判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案在江苏省邳州市法院开庭审理，次日，因辩护人向法院提出了管辖权异议及请求排除非法证据、调取监视居住期间录像的申请，遂法庭只好宣布休庭。目前被羁押于江苏省邳州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_66.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_66.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王刚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1958</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，河北省人，原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授，人类党网站（或人类党论坛）作者<span lang="EN-US">, </span>笔名“诺亚方舟”，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。十几年前，曾因发表多篇评论时政及反思文革的文章，而被其任职大学所在地河北省邯郸市当局视为重点监控对像；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，又因质疑中共享人制度及专制腐败现像等，发表《致中共中央的公开信》，呼吁政治改革，而被邯郸市丛台区警方贴身监控；后因其不惧危险，仍旧经常在微信上发表批评政府的文章，而曾被邯郸市警方处治安拘留<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次（第一次拘留<span lang="EN-US">19</span>天，第二次拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天），被喝茶<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多次；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因再次呼吁中共反腐和政改等，后又于同年创立“上海百姓维权”与“中国百姓维权”等微信群，表明中共绝不会走民主宪政之路，故而呼吁“民众移民”，但此言行被警方获悉，遂立遭丛台区联西派出所警方的野蛮执法，并派专人以“科研助手”名义对其进行贴身监视；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，“六四”来临前夕，其频遭当地警方约谈和做笔录，并被威胁称，若其尽快退出微信群，且不再在网上发表违规言论，就不对其翻旧账，但若继续发声，不仅会被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10-15</span>天，更会将其以前的案子推翻，再以“颠覆国家政权罪”论处；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其突遭警方立案侦查，并由公安部统一部署，在全国五六个省份（如闽、粤、湘和海南等省） 对其展开调查；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被邯郸市丛台区丛西派出所警方以约谈之名诱骗至派出所后失联，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉，其已被邯郸市丛台区警方正式刑事拘留。目前被羁押于邯郸市第一看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉：因言获罪六四前遭中共当局以刑事拘留的原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授王刚涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日由邯郸市公安局移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被中共当局以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前在河北邢台监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/26.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/26.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/2022819.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/2022819.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_28.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_28.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王国廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，天津市人，原天津市北辰区下辛庄村民，维权者王复春之父，“夏俊峰”式的维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其所在村庄举行村干部换届选举，有“恶霸村长”之称的黄双来欲求连任，但却遭村民反对；鉴于黄在任期间存在帐目不清、多占土地等严重问题，村民决定推举其子王复春和另一村民衡庆杰竞选村官，随遭到黄双来等人的忌恨、威胁恐吓和打击报复。由于黄双来一直认为其子王复春的参选是受其指使，并唯恐王国廷为人正直，在村中有极高威望，会影响他的村长连任，随心生恶念，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日带领几名打手（据称皆系黄的亲戚）闯进其家中肆意打闹，其子王复春闻讯前来劝阻并报警，警方却不出警；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，黄再次指派打手前去暴打王复春，并用枪托将其嘴巴打伤，无奈之下王等人二次报警，警方依然既不出警也不立案；<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，黄第三次带领<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人夜闯其家，对其实施肆意殴打，其子女家人及众多村民纷纷赶往现场，双方发生冲突；尽管王等人立即报警，警方依然消极不作为，结果在正当防卫过程中，致使黄和另两名打手被钝器击伤、死亡；尽管之后其主动自首，但其及其亲友等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人均被警方抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，经天津市中级法院秘密审判，其被以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥夺政治权利终身；鉴于判决明显与事实不符，其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，天津市高级法院被迫对其进行两次秘审，仍做出宣判：“维持原判死刑，立即执行”；其不服继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰二人死刑复核通过并执行。王国廷重新庭审量刑。后王国廷被改判死缓。目前被羁押于天津市北辰看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王国辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王国辉和于春丽夫妇系山东省青岛市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，原住青岛市城阳区棘洪滩街道段家庄。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年因警方多次迫害，夫妇两人离家避祸。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，城阳区国保大队和棘洪滩派出所警察包围了王国辉、于春丽夫妇的租住处，将夫妇两人抓捕，先关押在派出所内几十天，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，于春丽、王国辉才被关押到普东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，王国辉、于春丽夫妇在青岛即墨区法院被庭审。当庭于春丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，王国辉被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。王国辉和于春丽当庭提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/4448.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/4448.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/25/%E9%9D%92%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%9B%BD%E8%BE%89%E5%92%8C%E4%BA%8E%E6%98%A5%E4%B8%BD%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E5%90%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E4%BD%99-467471.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/25/%E9%9D%92%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%9B%BD%E8%BE%89%E5%92%8C%E4%BA%8E%E6%98%A5%E4%B8%BD%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E5%90%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E4%BD%99-467471.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 297.0pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王颢达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁吉林辽源公民。香港人民的反送中运动实际上得到许多大陆人民的支持，中共当局恐香港事态影响内地，一方面严密封锁消息，删帖删号封群，严密封杀消音；另一方面，对公开表达支持的网民则迅速抓捕，有的被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁吉林辽源公民王颢达在微博上发布蒙面、独眼，倒拿五星红旗，手持打火机的照片，随后即刻遭辽源警方抓捕刑拘。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功女学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生。法轮功女学员王红、董玉英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在鄠邑区将村镇附近讲真相时，被人恶意举报，被将村镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。王红因检查身体不适，被放回家。两人都被构陷到检察院、法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月西安市莲湖区法院非法庭审两名法轮功学员，王红坚持自己无罪，为自己做了有理有据的无罪辩护。王红保外就医在家，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日王红被蒋村镇派出所与鄠邑区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>警察在家绑架，现在被非法关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。后王红被西安市莲湖区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王红（重庆）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月生，重庆潼南区塘坝镇人，在重庆渝北区租房居住。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，王红开始修炼法轮功，为此王红曾被判刑四年、劳教一年——<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，王红用自己的电脑编辑打印了关于天安门自焚事件疑点的传单，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在看守所和监狱曾遭酷刑虐待。出狱后，流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，又被抓捕送北碚西山坪劳教所劳教一年，同样经过了长时间的酷刑折磨和每天的强制洗脑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，重庆市公安局渝北区分局警察闯入王红、戴淑芬的暂住处，将他们抓捕。王红和戴淑芬随后被关押到重庆市渝北区看守所。重庆市江北区法院<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，对王红、戴淑芳开庭，律师为他们作有理有据的无罪辩护。三个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，江北区法院宣判：判王红<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、戴淑芳<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，并罚金一万五千元。王红刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/986.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/986.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/3/%E9%87%8D%E5%BA%86%E7%8E%8B%E7%BA%A2%E3%80%81%E6%88%B4%E6%B7%91%E8%8A%B3%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464872.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/3/%E9%87%8D%E5%BA%86%E7%8E%8B%E7%BA%A2%E3%80%81%E6%88%B4%E6%B7%91%E8%8A%B3%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464872.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王洪兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古基督徒。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，自<span lang="EN-US">24</span>岁信主以来，一生都在侍奉教会。王洪兰等人因销售正规出版的圣经于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被抓捕，并被指控为非法经营罪。与王洪兰一起被抓捕的还有王洪兰的丈夫、王洪兰的二儿子以及已故大儿子的妻子等四人。王洪兰检察机关认定他们销售圣经的金额超过<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>万元，王洪兰作为第一被告检察院建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日获悉：王洪兰因销售正规出版圣经被抓捕案最近已召开了庭前会议，正式开庭定于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月下旬，拟开庭三周。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/4_28.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/4_28.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王洪霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省嫩江县九三农垦局荣军农场法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生。王洪霞、于桂荣<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日发放真相资料，被警察跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在于桂荣家被嫩江县公安局不法警察绑架，被关押到齐齐哈尔第二女子看守所。（这是王洪霞、于桂荣两人第二次同时遭绑架、构陷，被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她们两人被绑架，于桂荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，王洪霞当时也被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，黑龙江省嫩江县法院判处王洪霞<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王洪武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省日照市五莲县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，五莲县法轮功学员李凤英、郑允美在五莲县大郭村集讲法轮功时被警察抓捕。随后，警察去李凤英、郑允美住处抄家，抢走大法书籍、打印机、笔记本电脑、法轮功币、护身符、法轮功台历等物品。警察又抓捕了法轮功学员王世花、王洪武及流离失所的潍坊学员杨明珍。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员遭警察审讯后，均被关押到日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日五人均被五莲县法院判刑：李凤英<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，王洪武<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，杨明珍、郑允美<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王世花被<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/22/461141.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/22/461141.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王红霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，四川省资阳市安岳县人，绰号小莲、小梅、小吴、莲姐，安岳县安岳镇铁峰路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号居民，前安岳县教师进修学校英语教师，茶叶生意经营者，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信徒，中国在押良心犯。因信仰和长期锻炼、宣传法轮功屡遭四川当局的逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因锻炼法轮功而被资阳市当局以“利用邪教组织扰乱社会秩序”罪由分别劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年（三次共计<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年半），劳教期间曾屡遭酷刑折磨；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因外省法轮功友人到成都做茶叶经销考察，当与其会面时被突然出现的成都市便衣警察以“是吸毒犯”为借口强行带走，并先后送到新津洗脑班、二娥湖洗脑班关押；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被资阳市安岳县警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”予以逮捕，并关押于资阳市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被四川省资阳市简阳县法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经四川省资阳市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月；据悉，曾在狱中因绝食抗议而致身体枯瘦如柴，生命垂危；其家属探监权（含约见律师）等遭禁。目前在四川省成都女子监狱六监区服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王宏滨：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。一九七一年出生。因坚持信仰真善忍，遭到中共多次绑架，被非法劳教、非法判刑，共计冤刑逾二十年。他曾于一九九九年被劳教，刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，王宏滨遭抓捕后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，被关押在马三家监狱。出狱后仅四年，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，王宏滨再次遭绑架。当日他正在家睡觉，被闯入的双城公安局警察抓捕、抄家，之后又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。在监狱中这些年，王宏滨身体一直不好，近期血压高达<span lang="EN-US">280</span>～<span lang="EN-US">300</span>。有狱警捎信说：“王宏滨状况很不好，已经在安排自己的后事了。”家属找相关部门要求办理保外就医。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，监狱七监区赵姓队长给家属来电话声称，他们没有迫害王宏滨，让他去医院看病他不配合。而据出狱犯人提供的信息，在监狱，王宏滨被迫害得非常严重。在外界打电话和家属介入的情况下，六月六日，狱警带王宏滨去了公安医院，也没通知家属。七日，又转回呼兰监狱。王宏滨入狱三年多了，狱方一直不让家属探视和打电话，完全剥夺了监狱明文规定的在押人员及其家属的基本权利。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/12/444805.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/12/444805.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王厚积<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省大连法轮功学。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，在大连地区对法轮功学员的集中抓捕行动中，王厚积被八一路派出所警察抓捕。后悉，王厚积遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441619.html#22422221331-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441666.html#22422221331-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，，原是西安市户县惠安化工厂一民品分厂的技术骨干。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她开始修炼法轮功。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共发动对法轮功的迫害后，王华因坚守法轮信仰，屡遭中共人员迫害，她遭迫害经历计有：被劳教、判刑；被拘禁在拘留所、看守所、洗脑班；遭严重经济迫害，被开除、扣押工资及退休金等。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王华在户县草滩村讲法轮功时，被警察抓捕、抄家、关押在西安市三爻看守所构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被先莲湖区法院被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。她不服判决，已上诉至西安市中级法院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/29/453869.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/29/453869.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林图们市法轮功学员。王慧是一九九五年五月开始修炼法轮功的。一九九九年七月二十日中共开始镇压法轮功，迫害法轮功学员。王慧曾遭多次中共关押、酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，图们市法轮功学员王慧等多名法轮功学员，被图们市国保警察抓捕。被关押到当时图们市<span lang="EN-US">610</span>在五工村生态园办洗脑班，当时那里关押迫害了<span lang="EN-US">40</span>名左右的法轮功修炼者。王慧等三名法轮功学员后来被从图们洗脑班转到延吉进一步迫害。后王慧被图们市检察院构陷，被图们市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年被关押到吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/4_20.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王继武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨双城区韩甸镇工程号村法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">.2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被当地派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日遭双城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。王继武已上诉。据悉，王继武自被抓捕后，在双城区看守所一直绝食反迫害，人已瘦得脱形。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/28/461366.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王家芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州市白云区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北襄樊人，华中师范大学数学专业硕士，原广州大学数学系副教授。中共对法轮功的残酷迫害就开始了。王家芳因坚定信仰真善忍，曾被劳教两年、两次被判刑，累计冤狱逾<span lang="EN-US">15</span>载。她被关押于广州洗脑班、三水洗脑班、槎头劳教所（二年）、广州白云区看守所、广东省女子监狱（九年）等，多次被迫害得生命垂危。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被白云区公安分局警察抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王家芳不服判决上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/3/454449.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
