line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王迦勒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古呼和浩特市“基督徒销售圣经案”受害者。内蒙古呼和浩特市王洪兰等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名基督徒被指控涉嫌非法经营罪于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被抓捕，其获罪原竟然是因销售正规出版圣经而导致的，他们补贴国内基督徒买的圣经，都是南京正规出版，没有盈利，竟然还是被强行控罪非法经营。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日该案正式开庭过程中，庭审中代理律师们列举大量的事实，对公诉人的指控予以反驳，律师们并向合议庭严正声明：“公诉人指控的非法经营罪，主观方面要求是故意。如果合议庭拒绝了解被告人的信仰，就表明合议庭不准备了解被告人高买低卖圣经的真实目的，也就是说，合议庭不打算正确地适用非法经营罪。”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">此案中王洪兰、季合营（王洪兰的丈夫）、季国龙（王洪兰的儿子）、王迦勒（王洪兰的侄子）、刘敏娜（姑娘）、刘伟（刘敏娜丈夫）、张旺、杨志军、李超等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人，被控涉嫌非法经营罪于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>被呼和浩特市回民区公安分局刑事拘留。除李超在羁押一年后被取保候审以外，其他人羁押期限已超过了两年零七个月，严重超过法定期限。目前仍被羁押<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/9.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/9.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王健：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市法轮功学员，女，一九八九年出生，兰州交通大学本科生，她毕业后任哈尔滨铁路集团公司宾县分公司助理工程师。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，王健从宾县家中去上班，被铁路公安局、宾县公安局国保大队和胜利街派出所的警察抓捕，她家中的笔记本电脑、打印机、大法书籍、手机等被抄走。她被关押在哈尔滨第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，王健被依兰县检察院批捕。后遭起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚款十万元。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被哈尔滨市中级法院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王健被关押到黑龙江女子监狱八监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/2.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/2.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/5/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E5%B9%B4%E8%BD%BB%E5%A5%B3%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E5%8B%92%E7%B4%A2%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%87%E7%BD%9A%E9%87%91-467885.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/5/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E5%B9%B4%E8%BD%BB%E5%A5%B3%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E5%8B%92%E7%B4%A2%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%87%E7%BD%9A%E9%87%91-467885.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建兵</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年生，甘肃天水人，独立公益人。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年大学毕业后，便加入北京西部阳光农村发展基金从事农村发展工作，开启长期关注青少年教育及成长的公益职业生涯。曾担任西部阳光基金会农村教育项目主管<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年加入广州恭明社会组织发展中心，作为青少年成长项目和残障社群赋能项目主管及统筹，支持和发起相关社区项目工作。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年起开始关注职业病工人的权益倡导和服务性工作，提供必要的法律支持。王也是国内<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>运动中重要的支持者。王建兵原计划<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日送别女权记者黄雪琴经香港赴英国留学。但是，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">,</span>广州警方于王建兵出租屋中<span lang="EN-US">(</span>位于广州海珠区新港西路<span lang="EN-US">)</span>强行将王建兵和即将出国留学的黄雪琴一同抓走<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并查抄了两人的私人财物。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">,</span>王建兵的朋友于黄埔长洲用于储物的出租屋也遭到警方强行撬锁进入搜查<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并带走大量物品和行李箱。据知情人士透露，目前可以确认两人系被广州警方控制，警方均以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”拘留了王建兵和黄雪琴两人<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并疑对双方采取了“指定居所监视居住”措施。主要原因是涉及日常在王建兵他家中的朋友聚会。警方拒绝告知亲友二人具体下落。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建兵家属收到广州市公安局发出的“逮捕通知书”，逮捕公函号为特殊的穗公捕通字<span lang="EN-US">[2021]X2</span>。该通知书显示王建兵已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被广州市公安局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权”的名义被执行逮捕。黄雪琴、王建兵于<span lang="EN-US"> 2022 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 27 </span>日正式移送广州市检察院审查起诉。此前黄雪琴曾在未通知家属与律师的情况下，被私下转移至疑似广州第二看守所处单独关押审讯数月，而王建兵也曾被单独关押于其他场所审讯数月。目前二人已重新转至广州第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_1.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，大庆油田总医院职工，家住大庆市萨尔图区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被大庆市萨尔图区铁人公安分局便衣警察抓捕，关押在大庆市第二看守所，遭构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年并罚款三万元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>初，王建辉被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱八监区。遭酷刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王建敏</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山东省烟台地区莱阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，山东烟台莱阳市柏林庄卫生院退休医生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，王建敏在莱阳市联通公司大门东侧邮箱投递法轮功信后，被莱阳公安跟踪绑架。傍晚，王建敏被抄家，警察抢走了大量私人物品，包括真相币、真相资料、电脑、打印机等，具体数目不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建敏即被关押到烟台市看守所，刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王建敏被莱阳市公安局非法逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，烟台市中级法院一审判王建敏<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏维权人士。王杰是宁夏特色硒砂瓜种植专业户，也是宁夏中宁县云鹏瓜果专业合作社硒砂瓜种植的内部承包人（股东），受经营部法人代表朱万云委托，就中宁县白马乡政府借国家领导人“退耕还林”、及“金山银山不如绿水青山”的讲话精神，以各种各样的违法手段破坏农业生产行为，多次到农村农业部、国家信访局等投诉反映，而中宁县公安局之前一直插手这种非警务事务，对他的依法维权行为实施打击报复。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚，宁夏维权人士王杰在北京大红门遭遇暴力截访，王杰行使正当防卫权利后报警，辖区大红门派出所以“故意伤害”传唤了王杰。随即移送了王杰当地警方中卫市公安局沙坡头区分局，当地警方立即对其以“涉嫌妨害公务罪”刑事拘留。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/blog-post_13.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/blog-post_13.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; minor-fareast;">王进仓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃省天水市甘谷县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，家住甘谷县新兴镇七甲村。王进仓于一九九九年七月之前修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，甘谷县国保大队闯入王进仓家院中将其抓捕，并对王进仓殴打，之后将王进仓关押到清水看守所。之后甘谷县国保大队将王进仓构陷到检察院，并将他转关到甘谷县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，天水市秦州区法院庭审王进仓，对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，他被转监到兰州市大沙坪监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王金凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。因坚持修炼法轮功，王金凤多次遭到中共迫害，被长期骚扰、拘留、洗脑班迫害，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被康平县法院判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在辽宁省女子监狱关押期间，王金凤遭到各种酷刑虐待和非人折磨。王金凤和李凤芝于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被皇姑区黄河派出所、皇姑区国保警察抓捕构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，沈阳市两位善良妇女王金凤、李凤芝坚持修炼法轮大法真、善、忍，被于洪区法院判刑：王金凤<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，李凤芝<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，各罚金五千元。王金凤刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/4/450397.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/4/450397.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王金荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大兴安岭地区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生，家住黑龙江大兴安岭地区松岭区小扬气镇。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，王金荣被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月得知，她被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被关押到黑龙江女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/7/31/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F65%E5%B2%81%E7%8E%8B%E9%87%91%E8%8D%A3%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-%E5%B7%B2%E5%85%A5%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1-463609.html"><b minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王景翠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大庆油田公司采油五厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已八十岁。原大庆石油管理局申大公司职工家属，家住红岗区采油五厂。她于一九九八年修炼法轮功，身心受益。一九九九年七月二十日，中共疯狂打压法轮功，残酷迫害法轮功修炼者；王景翠曾多次被绑架、抄家、关押，经济勒索、一次被劳教，三次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被红岗区公安分局警察抓捕，被大庆市萨尔图区高新开发区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款一万元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年过完年，她被转入到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害，这已是她第三次被诬判入狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/13/444853.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/13/444853.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王景丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">哈尔滨市双城区人，法轮功学员。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年对法轮功的迫害过程中，她曾在看守所、劳教所、洗脑班、派出所被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区公安分局建国派出所抓捕抄家，被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所；当天哈尔滨南岗区、道里区、道外区、香坊区、松北区、双城区<span lang="EN-US">17</span>名法轮功学员被警察抓捕、抄家、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王聚才<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后王聚才被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，王聚才刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王军平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北石家庄市鹿泉区石井乡栈道村维权人士。因王军平的工人被无缘无故居打成重伤，王军平自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>起到北京中南海周边上访<span lang="EN-US">13</span>次拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，王军平去镇政府上访，镇长让司机开车离开，王军平到镇长车前要求镇长答复，镇长的司机就殴打王军平。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，王军平在亲戚家被欺骗回家以寻衅磁事刑事拘留，后被起诉。此案<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日在法院开庭，未判决。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span minor-fareast;">王君洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁康平县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，家住辽宁省沈阳市康平县东关乡。在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安。因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。王君洲在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日（或<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日）下班时，被滨新区生态城分局警察抓捕，据说是因为在微信中转发香港反送中相关信息。在王君洲被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被天津市滨海新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王克民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王兰英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">安徽省阜阳市临泉县法轮功学员。王翠兰、王翠萍、王兰英、李海涛等人，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被临泉县法院秘密开庭、判刑和经济罚款。王兰英遭临泉县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日送往安徽省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/12/451806.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王蕾</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：女 ，北京西城区法轮功学员。王蕾因发放法轮功材料，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午其家被西城派出所和国保抄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，王蕾北京西城区德胜门外派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日二次开庭。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，二审维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/24/459144.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/24/459144.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王立芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王复春的母亲。因竞选村长，原天津下辛庄村恶霸村长黄双来对村民王复春参与竞选恨之入骨，多次带领亲信打手到王复春父母家逼其退选，二老也曾多次报警警方不管。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日夜间<span lang="EN-US">11</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点钟，黄双来带<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人夜闯王国廷家，暴力威胁王国廷，不准其子王复春参选村长，与闻讯赶来的王复春及众村民发生冲突，黄双来等三人被殴致死。该案<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日一审，天津一中院将“聚众斗殴罪”改为“故意杀人罪”判处王复春、王国廷、村民衡庆杰死刑，王立芳被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰死刑通过并执行。王立芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王立恒</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">:1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，山东省淄博市桓台县人，淄博市桓台县果里镇马王村<span lang="EN-US">187</span>号公民；香港占中运动支持者，“恶俗维基”及“支纳维基”二网站骨干成员，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年期间，其因与多人积极合作组建“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”二网站，随深受网站友人好评；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因香港“占中”、要求“真普选”运动遭到中共当局授意下的港府严打，同时中国大陆《人民日报》又连续第<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天刊文批评占中运动，随于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日毅然赴香港金钟占领区，在天桥顶撑伞支持“占中”的学生及市民；但返回后不久，即被淄博市桓台县警方刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又被山东省桓台县检察院以涉嫌“非法获取公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“侵犯公民个人信息罪”和“非法获取国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因其又重回恶俗维基网站工作，而此时已有多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的信息（含户籍和照片等个人信息），其所在“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”网站亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂立遭中共当局的打压迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部迅速成立项目组，要求对全国该网站会员实施大抓捕；之后经严格审讯，发觉他们年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，故而各地警方将所抓之人纷纷予以释放，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把该警局所属的网站会员（含其在内）尽都抓捕，并上报公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被广东省茂名市警方跨省抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等转刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪、侵犯公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；据悉曾因资料不足，而被检察院几次退侦和被地方法院数次退回要求重新起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”被广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，王立恒被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年），“侵犯公民个人信息罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月），二罪并罚，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；其等均表不服，已经上诉；二审维持原判。目前王立恒被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王立群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃庆阳市庆城县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，甘肃庆阳庆城县驿马镇个体户，一九九四年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共迫害法轮功后，王立群坚持法轮功信仰，多次遭当地中共人员骚扰、迫害，曾被劳教三年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，王立群因向最高法院、最高检察院控告江泽民的罪状遭到当地“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、公安局的追捕而被迫远走他乡。王立群一直被通缉，庆阳市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”为了抓捕王立群，在网上对他通缉，把他的照片放在“天网”的云数据库里，跟全国各地的摄像头连接，只要他出现在联网摄像头内，通过<span lang="EN-US">AI</span>人脸识别就可以很快确认他的身份、确定他所出现的位置。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，王立群在西安一家商场干活，在换衣间换工服的时候取下了口罩，被摄像头拍到，暴露了行踪，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日遭庆阳市庆城县国保大队警察抓捕，被押回了庆阳市庆城县，关押在庆城县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，王立群被庭审。后王立群被庆阳市镇原县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南洛阳法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。其丈夫李树林：河南洛阳法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁，均为洛阳市涧西区退休人员。早年修炼法轮功后。一九九九年七月中共疯狂迫害法轮功后，李树林自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年间被<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次抓捕至洗脑班关押、恐吓、打骂，两次被拘留。在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年过年期间，李树林、王丽娟夫妇给人发放法轮功资料时，被人举报，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被洛阳市涧西区公安分局政保警察闯进家中抓捕并抄家。后二人被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>～<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，李树林、王丽娟夫妇失踪，近日被法院秘密判刑，李树林被判刑四年，王丽娟被判刑五年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王丽珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年出生，山东省淄博市人，淄博市张店区刘家村公民，强拆受害者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其父母家曾因遭当地政府强拆，家产被抢劫，房屋变废墟，其父母辛苦一辈子的成果一夜全无，遂其父亲王玉杨被迫上访，但结果是不仅各项维权要求未被解决，返遭当地政府捏造罪名枉法构陷，被淄博市张店区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；其母亦被列为网上逃犯，逃亡在外不敢回家；为讨公道和追回家产，其开始替父伸冤，上访维权，期间，因屡次维权投诉并数次围观、发视频声援其他与自家相类似的强拆受害事件，遂屡遭政府打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因在网上曝光“淄博开发区强拆事件”（即当地村民为抗强拆，手拿<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个煤气罐和多个酒瓶与警方对恃，情况十分紧急），而被潍坊市张店区警方带走传唤，后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，曾因其父举报官员非法强拆，多年上访而无果反被构陷入狱，遂其不得不向社会发出求助视频，但此举立遭打击，其家多日半夜被警察敲门恐吓、骚扰，并被断电；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，因其父家房产遭政府强拆已达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年问题一直不予解决，故而录制视频进行控诉，以期引起社会各界关注，解决实际问题，遂其将视频发到各微信群，寻求声援和呼吁；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其即被淄博市张店区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”带走、刑拘。目前被羁押于淄博市看守所（山东省淄博市张店区傅家镇傅家村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">255022</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王连荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市西青区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，一九九七年十二月开始修炼法轮功。因坚持修炼法轮功曾经两次遭冤狱迫害——<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年遭抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在天津女子监狱遭虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年又遭抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。王连荣于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被天津市西青区张家窝派出所警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，其被西青法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/4_13.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/4_13.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员，男。于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功起，王林曾多次被中共邪党抓捕、关押，在拘留所，看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受酷刑折磨。本次王林是于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被锦州市公安局高新区分局警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被锦州凌海市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金八千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。信<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/17/463069.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/17/463069.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王琳琳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名‘我在红尘你在天上<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>’。女，安徽人士，徽乡网总监，因于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<span lang="EN-US">15</span>时通过新浪微博发布消息称：安徽颖上夏桥镇拆迁逼死老人，发微博的同时附有一段十秒钟显示，视频中显示有多名身着“特警”字样服装的彪形大汉，队形整齐，臂戴红色袖套，蒙着黑色头套，到一处疑似办丧事的地方“执法”。该视频早前已被微博官方删除。后王琳琳于在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索未遂”罪抓捕关押，后王琳琳因揭发熊德超领导下的颍上拆迁逼死老人、美好乡村虚假惠民工程，而被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。此案正在申诉中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王楣泓<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省牡丹江市法轮功学员，牡丹江市地质勘察所高级工程师，丈夫于宗海是画家，就职于牡丹江市图书馆。夫妻俩因修炼法轮功曾被判十多年。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，王楣泓被牡丹江市爱民区中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害，曾多次遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日又被哈尔滨市南岗区公安分局哈西派出所警察抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院庭审。后获悉，王楣泓被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初投入黑龙江女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：湖南省衡阳市衡山县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份王梅英在广州大学城发法轮功资料，被监控器监视到。<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日王梅英被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b lang="EN-US">14</span>日晚上，孙雪冰、王敏夫妻被长春市二道区杨家店派出所抓捕，被关押在兴隆山看守所构陷迫害。王敏被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被劫持到吉林省女子监狱迫害。她丈夫孙雪冰被判两年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王明海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，遂遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，突遭冲击，被芜湖市戈江区警方闯入教学点，将包括其在内的十名老师悉数带走，教学点亦遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其十人被视为同案犯，统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被取保候审外，王明海及万红霞等另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名老师均被芜湖市戈江区检察院以同罪由正式批捕；据悉，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王明慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省雅安市名山区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日晚王明慧被名山区国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。后被关押在雅安天全看守所。王明慧于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，索罚金一万元。近两年后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被关押到成都龙泉驿女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王明全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃省庆阳市环县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，身心受益。王明全<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被环县环城派出所警察从家中抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，王明全被环县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林省舒兰市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年近七十岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，王朋影多次被绑架，曾三次被劳教，一次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王朋影出门办事，被警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所迫害。后获悉，王朋影被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林长春法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林市桦甸人，男，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生。一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。一九九七年，王鹏毕业后分配到吉林化纤厂二氧化硫车间，先后被评为先进工作者和标兵。自从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共江泽民集团镇压法轮功后，王鹏因坚持修炼，屡遭邪恶迫害——被吉林化纤厂开除；在桦甸市公安局遭受酷刑折磨；曾被抓捕、判刑六年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，长春净月彩宇大街派出所将其抓捕，随后，王鹏被刑事拘留，关押在长春市公安监管中心（苇子沟看守所）。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，王鹏被宽城区法院以疫情为由到看守所开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月年获悉，王鹏被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/3/456389.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王鹏义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁王。王鹏义是军队转业干部，在军队为国家服务多年，转业到抚顺市粮食局所属企业。在中共江泽民集团发动的对法轮功的迫害<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年中，王鹏义遭受了多次抓捕、劳教、判刑，受到多种酷刑折磨，九死一生，身心受到极大的伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，王鹏义失踪，经常与他在一起的亲友也联系不上他。一年半以后获悉，他又被抚顺市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在在沈阳沈北新区康家山监狱二监区。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王平创：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市武功县法轮功学员。王平创<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，妻子赵西娟<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日生，陕西咸阳市武功县普集镇义老村人，近年在西安做生意维持生活。王平创曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被劳教迫害，在枣子河劳教所受尽酷刑，被关笼子、夏天暴晒、冬天被浇凉水、做奴工、被牢头暴打等，他一度被迫害致生命垂危。由于警察多次上门骚扰，王平创夫妻被迫流离失所在外。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，王平创夫妻骑电动车在本市公交站牌上粘贴“法轮大法好”，遭人举报。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日夫妻俩遭周至县公安局和长安区郭杜镇派出所抓捕，参与的警察有<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多人，并抄家。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span>王平创、赵西娟夫妇在西安遭抓捕关押构陷近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">, </span>于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被雁塔区法院法官分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，共勒索<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万惩金。两人不服判决，已上诉至西安市中级法院。目前王平创被关押在西安市安康医院，赵西娟被关押在西安市看守所，两处均以疫情为由不让会见。王平创刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-%E7%8E%8B%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%9B%E3%80%81%E8%B5%B5%E8%A5%BF%E5%A8%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-441327.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-%E7%8E%8B%E5%B9%B3%E5%88%9B%E3%80%81%E8%B5%B5%E8%A5%BF%E5%A8%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-441327.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王齐花：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年六十六岁，家住武汉市新洲区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日上午十点多钟，村部会计何胜伢带领新洲区国保大队四人和旧街派出所一人，闯入王齐花家中，非法抄家，其中一人带着摄像机在家里到处摄像，来人看到王齐花家里挂的匾额十字绣艺术品（绣有法轮大法好和莲花），就强行摘下带走，还搜出几部旧手机，这群人就走了。后被新洲区国保大队和当地警察绑架到蔡甸区玉笋山洗脑班，几天后关到第一女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，武汉新洲区法院判王齐花八年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王强：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1993</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，山西省人，山西省临汾市荛都区基督徒，临汾市基督教圣约家园教会同工，中国在押良心犯。因其所在教会属于基督教归正家庭教会，且因其等教会神职人员、同工及众信徒拒不愿加入中共“三自”教会，遂自新宗教事务条例实施以来，其所在教会即成为当局屡加迫害的家庭教会之一；在逼迫中，不仅教会时常被民宗局官员带着多人前来骚扰、威胁和冲击，其作为同工亦成为山西当局维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因其参与教会在户外举办的<span lang="EN-US">70</span>人的“亲子营”活动，突遭当地警方<span lang="EN-US">100</span>余人的围堵和冲击，并将包括其在内的所有现场参与者悉数带走，教会物品被查抄，教会神职人员李洁和韩晓栋等人被临汾市警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住，后又转为刑拘、逮捕，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，也被临汾市警方拦截、抓捕，并于次日被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住；七天之后（即<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日），又被临汾市警方以同罪由转为刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，知其所在临汾圣约家园教会和阿斯兰学堂已被临汾市尧都区民政局正式在政府官网发布公告取缔，但其个人更多讯息尚不知情。目前被羁押于山西省尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_77.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_77.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王清：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>河南省南阳市人，政府信息公开申请人，知名民间维权举报打假人，中国在押维权人士。十多年前，曾因向河南省南阳市“<span lang="EN-US">181</span>个政府部门申请信息公开”，引起社会热议，但被官方视为“河南刁民”；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，又曾因举报打假而被网络评选为“<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年十大公民”之一，自此其维权行为更是全国闻名；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因将有官方支持背景，且有违法经营操作的南阳市逸美时光咖啡店投诉到当地工商管理部门，期间虽经两次调解未果，但在其不懈努力下，最终迫使工商机关依法对该店做出罚款<span lang="EN-US">45000</span>元措施，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年向当地法院提出予以强制执行申请；然而其正义维权行为却因触碰了当地权贵集团的利益，遂遭官商勾结势力的打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，后被卧龙区检察院快速批捕，并被指控，因其在向各级工商管理部门进行投诉举报时有“威胁恐吓敲诈勒索商家”之嫌，故而触犯了政府相关法律；另有陈强、王聚才及韩猛等三名维权打假者亦作为同案犯被相继逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，另三人亦被分别枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年不等，并处罚金若干；其不服判决，立即提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，经南阳市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，目前被羁押于南阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王秋萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。因修炼法轮功，王秋萍曾经被关押在马三家劳教所迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因发放疫情周刊被一位武警恶告。送到马路湾派出所，搜走了随身带的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>千多元钱和手表、自行车和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>张封城期间的某小区通行证。由两个和平区国保大队的人连打带骂的审问，王秋萍不配合迫害，没报名，没签字，半夜逃走。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，再次被抓捕，送往和平区精神病院迫害。王秋萍被关押在精神病院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个半月多后，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被和平区国保大队、马路湾派出所警察送往沈阳市第二看守所迫害。看守所拒绝家人送衣物、存钱，更不许律师接见。王秋萍<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被关押到辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/10/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436647.html#2219223842-5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/10/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436647.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王荣军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1950</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年七十二岁；女儿那艳四十多岁，是沈阳市第六医院的护士。王荣军、那艳母女俩于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日左右失踪。亲朋好友到处寻找，从那艳工作单位，到派出所，到街道，没有任何人提供讯息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，亲属才得到母女俩被绑架并被判刑的确切消息。现在她们仍被非法关押在沈阳市第一看守所。王荣军及女儿那艳（那燕）已分别被辽中区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/22/443930.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/22/443930.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王容媛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林辽源市东丰县法轮功学员。王容媛<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚发放法轮功资料时，被警察抓捕到派出所，掰坏了她的胳膊。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，派出所警察到王容媛居住的地方搜走资料、电脑、打印机、刻录机、横幅机器等受法律保护的私人财物。王容媛当天被送往辽源市拘留所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，家属去接人没接到。她被派出所警察先劫持回东丰镇派出所，当天晚上又给送到辽源市看守所继续关押。后获悉，王容媛被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月送往吉林省女子监狱，至今不让她家属接见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/15/457753.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/15/457753.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王瑞玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日王瑞玲被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王瑞伶于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被关押于河北女子监狱，遭到强迫抠嘴灌药，揪头发撞墙，往身上浇凉水等迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月已经生命垂危。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日傍晚，北京朝阳区大屯派出所警察到王润荣家抄家，并抓捕了王润荣。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前被关押在顺义区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/30/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%B0%AD%E5%AE%88%E7%A4%BC%E3%80%81%E8%83%A1%E9%94%A6%E5%87%A4%E7%AD%89%E4%BA%94%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-466607.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/30/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%B0%AD%E5%AE%88%E7%A4%BC%E3%80%81%E8%83%A1%E9%94%A6%E5%87%A4%E7%AD%89%E4%BA%94%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-466607.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王四美<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。王四美刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王尚杰：男，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波<span lang="EN-US">,4</span>人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判王尚杰<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王胜利：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，内蒙古自治区人，原中共党员，前内蒙古自治区公安厅刑事侦查总队警察，内蒙古自治区公安厅经济犯罪侦查总队侵害知识产权市场秩序犯罪侦查支队原支队长，蒙冤维权警察，反腐举报人。早年曾就读于内蒙古医科大学，但毕业后并未从事医生职业，而是选择继承父业，通过公务员考试进入公安系统成为一名刑侦警察；工作中，因曾侦办过许多大案要案，故而多次获得一等功、二等功、三等功等殊荣，并被评为内蒙古自治区优秀侦查员；然而，因其工作岗位的特殊性及其工作态度的敬业、认真性，让其看到经济案件侦查工作的复杂性与在巨额利益驱使下的人性脆弱、丑陋的一面；自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年始，因拒绝与其上司王来明（内蒙古自治区公安厅原党委副书记、副厅长，以下简称“王”，已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日因涉嫌严重违纪违法而落马）媾和，利用职权助其贪污腐败、图谋私利，随成为王以案谋私的“挡路石”和仇视对象；后其虽对王之要求尽量选择疏远和回避，但终致被制造冤案，遭遇戕害；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被准格尔旗监察委员会以“因曾侦办过‘<span lang="EN-US">9.18</span>项目’（即王玉宝、常青等人合同诈骗案），有被‘保护伞’用以为此案犯罪嫌疑人‘做翻案工具’之嫌”为由带走，采取留置措施；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案被准格尔旗监委会以涉嫌“贪污、受贿和挪用公款”三罪向准格尔旗检察院提起审查起诉，之后曾被准格尔旗检察院以同罪由转正式批捕，但又因案件证据不足，曾有两次将其案退回侦补，三次延长审理起诉期限；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案再次被移送检察院审查起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被自治区公安厅党委开除党籍、开除公职；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其案被准格尔旗检察院以涉嫌“贪污、挪用公款、受贿、巨额财产来源不明、滥用职权”等五罪向准格尔旗法院提起公诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被内蒙古自治区准格尔旗法院一审以“受贿罪；挪用公款罪、巨额财产来源不明罪、贪污罪；滥用职权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，立即提起上诉，坚称其所谓“罪行”并非真实，皆是“办案人员严刑逼供、编造罗织的产物”；后经鄂尔多斯市中级法院二审裁决，宣布撤销原一审判决，将案件发回重审；同时，因其身体极差，生命随时面临危险，随迫不得已准于取保候审出狱；但其为讨回公道，昭雪冤屈，一边取保在外治病，一边在网上发控诉信和遗书，公开举报王来明，称他才是纪检内鬼和真正的犯罪分子，并在幕后指使，致其终身残疾；同时，还通过各种合法途径持续向相关部门提交近<span lang="EN-US">80000</span>份《控告信》、《举报信》，虽都石沉大海，了无果效，但依然对外表明其已做好准备，誓将《遗书》、《控告信》和《举报信》留给家人、组织及社会，故而很快即被准格尔旗看守所收监；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案经鄂尔多斯中级法院三审，仍以受贿罪（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年），巨额财产来源不明罪（<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月），贪污罪<span lang="EN-US"> (1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">),</span>最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日；据悉，其母张仙花和两名亲戚因为其喊冤，竟也都被准格尔旗当局以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”拘捕；其中，其母于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被枉判刑期<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、缓期执行<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前被羁押于内蒙古自治区准格尔旗看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王世花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省日照市五莲县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，五莲县法轮功学员李凤英、郑允美在五莲县大郭村集讲法轮功时被警察抓捕。随后，警察去李凤英、郑允美住处抄家，抢走大法书籍、打印机、笔记本电脑、法轮功币、护身符、法轮功台历等物品。警察又抓捕了法轮功学员王世花、王洪武及流离失所的潍坊学员杨明珍。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员遭警察审讯后，均被关押到日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日五人均被五莲县法院判刑：李凤英<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，王洪武<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，杨明珍、郑允美<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王世花被<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/22/461141.html"><b mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王淑波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市嘉荫县嘉荫农场退休职工，户籍所在地黑龙江省嘉荫县嘉荫农垦社区<span lang="EN-US">B</span>区<span lang="EN-US">9</span>委<span lang="EN-US">1</span>组<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功，王淑波于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日傍晚，在佳木斯市住处遭向阳公安分局松林派出所警察入室抓捕、关押构陷，两次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，佳木斯市向阳区法院对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其被关押在佳木斯市看守所。王淑波上诉到佳木斯市中级法院，中院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被关押至黑龙江女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%8E%9F%E4%BC%8A%E6%98%A5%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E6%B3%A2%E5%9C%A8%E4%BD%B3%E6%9C%A8%E6%96%AF%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434327.html"><b
