mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王淑华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林松原市法轮功学员。为营救丈夫——松原市法轮功学员李国军，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日王淑华到长春市民康路派出所去要人，被非法扣押。后来得知王淑华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日送到兰家女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王淑云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日在街上宣传法轮功，被站前派出所警察抓捕，被关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月她家属得知，王淑云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金两万元。法院开庭没有通知她家属。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E5%96%84%E4%BC%A0%E9%81%BF%E7%96%AB%E8%89%AF%E6%96%B9-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E4%BA%91%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-441353.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/16/%E5%96%84%E4%BC%A0%E9%81%BF%E7%96%AB%E8%89%AF%E6%96%B9-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E6%B7%91%E4%BA%91%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-441353.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王素平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王铁壮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，原南阳市工商局局长，法轮功学员。一九九九年七月法轮功被迫害后，当时法轮功学员王铁壮想为法轮功说句公道话，于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年进京上访，被当地公安接回后，南阳市市委书记、公安局长亲自作“转化”。他坚持法轮功，中共决定劳教他三年，把他关入河南省第三劳教所。南阳市政法委、公安局从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初对法轮功学员进行监听、监控，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份开始对全市所有住户、门店等进行名为入户走访，其实质是进入法轮功学员家中要户口簿、身份证、填表登记、照相。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日凌晨开始，在南阳市区以及各县开始大面积抓捕。王铁壮于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日也被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月王铁壮被南阳市宛城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王伟才：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省人，佛山市顺德区公民，基督徒，曾为个体经商者，后为广东顺德盛佳家庭教会全职服事同工，“盛佳共学互助中心”培训员，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年皈依基督教以来，因秉承信仰，诚心参与教会聚会、敬拜活动并经常帮助教友排忧解难，而深得教牧同工及教友们的喜爱；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因其立定全身心投入福音的传播活动，故而毅然放下自己的生意而在顺德盛佳家庭教会做全职服事同工；因其在教会从事同工活动过程中，认识到盛佳教会虽属家庭教会，但在法律上却是受国家宗教自由白皮书明文保护的合法教会，并且其教会内部印刷的一些与圣经相关培训学习数据也不未违法，遂经常向教会信徒及其亲友、慕道友（即常到教会听道，但未受洗的信仰追求者）等人推介和共同学习这些与圣经根本不违背的内部数据；然而近年来，因中共当局修订并强化了对《宗教事务条例》的管理，佛山市民宗局遂频繁前往盛佳家庭教会，要求教会加入和接受中共所属的“三自教会”管辖，但因被其等教牧同工多次拒绝，遂屡遭地方当局上门骚扰、警告；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，盛佳教会开设的“盛佳共学互助中心”（即圣经学习培训班）突遭顺德区警方、民宗局和小区人员等数十人的联合查处，教会所用教学设备及学习数据全被没收，教会大门被查封，其与传道人邓燕祥和教会同工朱江龙、朱巧玲等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被警方带走；次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日），其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均被顺德区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其等又被顺德区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控他们因让教会信徒和培训学生使用教会内部印刷的圣经学习数据，故此行为与国家新修订《宗教管理条例》相抵触，应被逮捕和法办；据悉，其被抓至今一直无更多解体信息，只知其家人生活、工作等面临极大压力，教会其余未被抓捕同工和信徒仍持续被警方约谈；又悉，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其教会朱龙飞长老也被顺德区警察以同罪名刑拘，并送同一看守所关押。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所（广东省佛山市南海区狮山镇招大（管理区）兴业东路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">528200</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/blog-post_55.html</span></b></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王卫真：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连法轮功学员、女、原沈阳军区大连高等医学专科学校内科教研室任教员，授衔上校，副师待遇。因坚持信仰、坚持讲法轮功真相，被中共当局多次骚扰、抓捕。每次抓捕都没有出示任何法律手续，比如搜查证等，完全是非法抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，在不通知任何亲属，法庭上只有陪送王卫真的儿子一人在场的情况下，中山区法院对她进行开庭审判。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，中山法院判王卫真<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年徒刑。后身体原因未入监。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，大连市中山区秀月派出所警察到家中抓捕了当时六十八岁的王卫真女士，将她强行劫持到大连市姚家看守所。人被送入看守所体检时，血压高至二百三十，但看守所仍然非法关押王卫真。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王卫真女士被押辽宁女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王文杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省秦皇岛市青龙县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共江泽民集团迫害法轮功后，她曾经多次遭受迫害，在<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年春被抓捕到青龙法制教育中心进行洗脑迫害，在烈日下暴晒等。王文杰于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被青龙县国保伙同木头凳镇派出所警察数人闯入家中抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王文杰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元<span lang="EN-US">.</span>。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/12/460180.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/12/460180.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王侠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省双鸭山市集贤县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，王侠（王霞）和牛玉杰两位女士在小区附近讲真相时，被不明真相世人举报，被福利派出所警察抓捕到派出所审讯、笔录。后王侠、牛玉杰二人被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被逮捕、关押在双鸭山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，集贤县法院对王侠、牛玉杰开庭，判王侠<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；牛玉杰<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月（经丈夫四处托人花了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万元，并代写“三书”，现期满回家。）。王侠刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王霞<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市东营法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，东营市公安局、分局、市国保支队、区国保大队及六户派出所、胜利派出所、新区派出所实施了抓捕，当时共有包括王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡在内的十多名法轮功学员被抓捕、抄家。其中，王霞因身体原因，被“取保候审”，崔桂芬、王沐怡两人被关押于东营市看守所。山东省东营市东营区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日对王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡进行开庭宣判。法官闫晓辉在没有任何法律依据的情况下对她们作出了非法判决。王霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款两万五千元；崔桂芬被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款两万元；王沐怡被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王晓翠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">又名王丽，黑龙江双鸭山市友谊县法轮功学员，女，一九六八年三月二日生。王晓翠<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在家中遭到抓捕、抄家，因身体原因第二天被“取保候审”。友谊县公安局与检察院、法院一直罗织“证据”，构陷她。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，友谊县政法委、公安局、检察院，法院诬陷王晓翠的图谋在明慧网上曝光，第二天王晓翠再次被友谊县公安局抓捕，据悉她被关押在双鸭山市集贤县看守所，属异地关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉王晓翠已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年底被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，目前关押地不详。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">205</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/24.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/24.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/3/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E5%8F%8B%E8%B0%8A%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%99%93%E7%BF%A0%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-467790.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/3/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E5%8F%8B%E8%B0%8A%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%99%93%E7%BF%A0%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-467790.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王晓光：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾市籍人，原山西师范大学公职人员，基督徒，山西省临汾市浮山县金灯堂家庭教会主要负责人、牧师，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">"9.13"</span>山西临汾教案受害人，中国在押良心犯。王晓光笃信基督<span lang="EN-US">;</span>早期曾在山西师范大学任职，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年起，离职开始全职在教会做服侍工作，后成为金灯堂家庭教会牧师与主要负责人<span lang="EN-US">;</span>曾因着有《十架神学》等十几 部基督教神学著作，对中国家庭教会进行了深入分析，并根据马丁·路德的十架神学，提出了中国家庭教会十架神学四条原则，故而在临汾家庭教会中备受尊重<span lang="EN-US">;</span>自<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年以来，在其夫妇（其妻子杨荣丽，同为金灯堂教会传道人和主要负责人）与教会其他同工的共同努力带领下，其教会从几十人发展成拥有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名基督徒的大型教会<span lang="EN-US">;</span>正是基于其教会及影响力越来越大，随引起地方政府的强烈不满和恐慌<span lang="EN-US">;</span>又因其教会拒绝到临汾市民宗局登记，接受中共<span lang="EN-US">"</span>三自教会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>的管理，随屡遭打压，其养老金和医保待遇等具被取消<span lang="EN-US">;2004</span>年始，教会经常被临汾市当局断水停电<span lang="EN-US">;2009</span>年，曾因众信徒奉献<span lang="EN-US">1700</span>万元人民币建造了金灯堂大教堂，但其地址却被 地方当局看好搞开发，并称给<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>万元收购金灯堂，被其夫妇等教会负责人断然拒绝，故立遭报复性打压<span lang="EN-US">;2009 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">9 </span>月，<span lang="EN-US">"9.13"</span>山西临汾教案发生<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其夫妇等教会<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被临汾市警方刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，案件被检察院迅速移交至法院<span lang="EN-US">;2009 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被临汾市尧都区法院统一宣判，其中，其被以<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法占用农用地罪<span lang="EN-US">" </span>和「聚众扰乱交通秩序罪」判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；随后，其教会<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多个聚会点全部被封<span lang="EN-US">;2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因其与教会神职人员及众信徒一直拒绝将金灯堂转让给地方政府，随被浮山县政府以强行爆破方式夷为平地<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，将其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>名教会神职人员和 同工悉数被抓捕，并被以金灯堂教会规模日益壮大，及家庭教会受洗不符国家规定等为由刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后部分人被取保释放，但其与其妻杨荣丽等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人仍被关押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被地方检察院以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>诈骗罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>予以批捕<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其案被移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">目前疑似被羁押于临汾市看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王新民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江牡丹江法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。原系黑龙江省烟草研究所高级农艺师，早在<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，因修炼法轮功，被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，关押在牡丹江监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，王新民被迫害出严重胰腺炎，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，被“保外就医”。在病情没有好转的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被牡丹江监狱以欺骗的手段，不顾身体情况，强行收监。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，才结束冤狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又被抓捕，关押在牡丹江看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被爱民区法院开庭，王新民为自己做了无罪辩护。后王新民被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年王新民被牡丹江中级法院驳回上诉，维护原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，王新民被劫持到牡丹江监狱集训队继续关押迫害。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，惠民县孙武镇马画村人。他因一直坚持法轮功信仰、向民众讲法轮功真相，多次遭中共公检法人员的骚扰、绑架、殴打、酷刑、关押、罚款、判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。王新忠<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日中午在家中被惠民县公安局国保大队警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被惠民县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王秀国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员。毕业于沈阳鲁迅美术学院，是一位心地善良的画家，家住抚顺市新抚区。因修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功的迫害中，他曾被判刑七年半。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，王秀国和孙晶，因在抚顺市顺城区前甸镇附近给民众介“法轮功，被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，各被罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/28/458206.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王秀英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：沈阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，一九九八年，王秀英开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，王秀英因向路人宣传法轮功，被于洪区城东湖派出所警察抓捕。年后获刑一年六个月，罚金五千元。王秀英于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日刑满释放回家。仅仅两年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，王秀英因宣传法轮功，再次被于洪区城东湖派出所警察抓捕，因血压超高、看守所拒收，次日，她被改成监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王秀英被于洪区检察院起诉至于洪区法院。于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被抓进沈阳市第一看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日王秀英被于洪区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。王秀英上诉到沈阳市中级法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，二审法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/4_8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王秀芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">内蒙古赤峰市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。因为坚持修炼法轮功、说真话，王秀芳曾多次被中共当局抓捕，两次遭判刑（累计刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年多）、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次遭劳教迫害，共<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年又加期<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，身陷囹圄共计<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年多。在这些年当中，她遭受到中共灭尽人性的迫害，被强制跪着、蹲着、撅着、掏镣子、开皮、坐铁椅子、背铐、吊铐、曝晒、强迫插管灌食、电棍电击、罚站、掐、踢、站马步、走鸭子步、跳蛤蟆步、不让睡觉、脱光衣服冷冻、逼迫把头扎到屎尿桶里、逼迫在太阳底下跳正步，被拳打脚踢是家常便饭，精神和肉体受到了极大的摧残和伤害，九死一生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日给人讲法轮功真相，遭人恶意举报，被抓捕、构陷，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现在正在上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/14/451893.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/14/451893.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王学勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省东营市胜利油田法轮功学员，胜利油田孤岛集输大队职工，五十多岁，性情温和，为人很热心，工作勤勉，家中有一位贤惠的妻子和一个非常孝顺的儿子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日中午，王学勇被河口公安分局孤岛派出所国保大队四个警察，其中两个穿警服、两个穿便衣，非法闯入家中抄家、绑架。后他被刑事拘留、关押于河口看守所，后又转入牛庄看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在家属不知道的情况下，被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。后被转入山东省监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王亚茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省四平市梨树县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王亚茹<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份发法轮功法轮功资料时，被梨树县公安局长抓捕，关押在四平看守所。王亚茹在看守所遭暴力殴打等非人道折磨。后被四平市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年被关押到吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/28/459300.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/28/459300.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王彦东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市绥中县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，绥中县国保大队副大队长刘唤宇等人，闯到高华家，抓捕了高华和高英姐妹，以及去串门的法轮功学员陈文艳和王彦东，抢劫了高华家的电脑、打印机等私人财物。高华被关押在葫芦岛看守所，高英被关押在葫芦岛拘留所，王彦东被关押在绥中看守所。陈文艳被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高华、高英、王彦东被构陷到绥中县检察院。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，高英回家，被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，高华、王彦东被构陷案到了葫芦岛连山检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日高华、王彦东被葫芦岛市连山法院判刑：高华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，王彦东<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；王彦东刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王彦辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省保定市清苑区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王彦辉在清苑区冉庄镇大张庄村集市上，散发法轮功资料，被人举报，被冉庄派出所警察抓捕。下午，王彦辉被带到清苑区公安局，因检体不合格，到傍晚被送回家。此后，王彦辉多次被抓捕，但因身体原因，均未被收监。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，王彦辉去清苑区公安局递送控告状，清苑区公安局推到检察院，检察院推到纪检委，纪检委推到信访局。当送到清苑区阳城镇派出所时，被阳城派出所抓捕。随后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，王彦辉家属接到王彦辉从监狱打来的电话才知道王彦辉已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被关押在河北省监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/3.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/2/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E4%BF%9D%E5%AE%9A%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E8%BE%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-466686.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/2/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E4%BF%9D%E5%AE%9A%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E8%BE%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-466686.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王怡：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，四川省三台县人，成都大学管理学院前讲师，“宪政论衡”网站创办人，作家，独立中文笔会会员，基督徒，成都秋雨圣约归正长老教会创办人、主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。早年间，曾创立主持宪政网络论坛，研究中国宪政转型，因经常发表文章政论文章，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年被中国大陆当时以敢言着称的《南方人物周刊》评为“最有影响力的公共知识分子”之一；后成为基督徒，创立秋雨圣约教会，但因拒绝加入中共管控的“三自教会”，且教会信徒与日俱增，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其欲出境参加一个香港的宗教会议时，竟被中国海关以“出境有可能危害国家安全”为由禁止出境；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其夫妇二人又被成都市警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由带走传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，成都秋雨圣约教会突然被成都市警方大规模夜袭，百余名基督徒被以涉“寻衅滋事”、“非法经营”等罪名抓走，其亦被传唤；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被成都市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；之后尽管秋雨圣约教会立即发起全球信徒禁食祷告行动，抗议中共当局打压宗教自由，但至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日仍被成都市警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；据悉，其在被捕前曾发声明称，当局若将罪名指向其信仰、写作、言论和传教行为，他“将一概予以否认，服刑而不服法，伏法而不认罪”；其所在成都秋雨圣约教会于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日随即被成都宗教事务管理局发文予以取缔。目前被羁押于成都市看守所（成都市郫都区安靖镇正义路<span lang="EN-US">3</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">611731</span>）。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被四川省成都市中级法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“非法经营罪”，二罪并罚，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王一飞：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，湖南省籍人士，化名小李，原网络秘密组织“兴中会”成员，网络秘密民运组织“兴华会”创建者和主要推动者，中国曾押政治犯。多年来一直低调并积极从事民主运动，因创建并与异议人士曾国凡等多人积极推动网络组织“兴华会”，倡导国内民众成立公民圈，开展启发民智的行动，而深受江西当局严控打压；因该会成员及支持者在南昌、赣州等地多处建筑物上喷涂“官员财产公开，人民代表直选”、“平反八九六四，结束一党专政”、“六四英灵，永远安息”等官方敏感标语，其宣传标语落款为“兴华会”，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其与曾国凡夫妇随被南昌市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”悉数带走、刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南昌市警方以同罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年某日，被江西省南昌市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江西南昌市洪都监狱服刑。王一飞<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日后微信朋友圈停止更新、微信公共号“一飞上天”则停在了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，最后一篇是“从看守所被解送到监狱服刑的纪念日”，至今失联一个多月，已遭抓捕。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/20_7.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈尔滨市双城区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。目前她被迫害致胸痛、腰椎间盘突出。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/10/450612.html#22109233444-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; minor-fareast;">王以诺：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽合肥基督教青年团契带领同工，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年生，男，未婚，老家在安徽利辛县。王以诺原来在西安华为公司工作，得知家乡许多年轻人到合肥读大学，辞去西安的工作回到安徽，在合肥市某公司上班。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年初在大学城成立“合肥青年团契”，开始的时候只有十几个人，迅速发展，到<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被冲击的时候，已经有将近两百人参加聚会，其中大部分是学生，少部分是已经工作的。合肥国保曾叫王以诺加入三自，或者去报备就可以了；王以诺没有答应。他们信徒的奉献都是通过微信转账，当时是考虑到比较方便，但是没有考虑到结果非常危险。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，“合肥青年团契”在聚会时被冲击，<span lang="EN-US">84</span>人当场被抓捕，警方押着王以诺到家里搜查，搜了几个小时，并没有搜查令也没有拘捕令，就把人抓走了。当天被抓的多数人<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时之后释放，有<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天后释放。被释放的人后来都没有什么事。主要同工王以诺、慕恩被刑拘，后被批准逮捕。家属在<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份收到通知，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉慕恩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元；王以诺弟兄被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/363.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">27</span>日被禹城市公安黑帮式抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被构陷至禹城检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被包头市东河区检察院起诉，经历三次开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，包头市东河区法院下达判决书，其中王鹰、张瑞童被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；孟丽丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被当地国保警察抓捕、构陷，一直被羁押在禹州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，王永胜被强制开庭，他女儿王洁和聘请的律师一起为王永胜作了无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，许昌魏都区法院法官判处王永胜有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金人民币三千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王钰超：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员。咸阳市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张鹏、王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏因为向淳化县民众发放真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月先后在各自的住所被淳化县公安局警察抓捕抄家。张鹏、王钰超（<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁左右）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底在咸阳市住处被警察绑架，电脑、打印机等设备被抢走。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位法轮功学员被关押在咸阳淳化县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均已被判刑，其中张鹏判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏约为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年不等，刑期不详。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王玉和：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省大连市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经八十二岁<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，王玉和因修炼法轮功，被判三年。当时在极大的压力下，王玉和出现了高血压和脑血栓两种高危病症，导致半身不遂，生活不能自理，被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，王玉和回到家中。此后，法院刑事庭庭长孙锡河接管王玉和案，再次下达收监令。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，大连市办案队警察闯到她女儿家，在王玉和独自在家之时，抓捕了她。被关押折磨一年半后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，家人探视发现王玉和身体虚弱，举步维艰，需要人搀扶。见此，女儿为已<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁的母亲申请保外就医，监狱拒收她的申请。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/26/%E4%B8%AD%E5%85%B1%E5%86%A4%E7%8D%84%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8%E5%85%AB%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E7%8E%89%E5%92%8C-%E5%AE%B6%E5%B1%AC%E7%94%B3%E8%AB%8B%E4%BF%9D%E5%A4%96%E5%B0%B1%E9%86%AB%E8%A2%AB%E6%8B%92%E6%94%B6-464587.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/26/%E4%B8%AD%E5%85%B1%E5%86%A4%E7%8D%84%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8%E5%85%AB%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E7%8E%89%E5%92%8C-%E5%AE%B6%E5%B1%AC%E7%94%B3%E8%AB%8B%E4%BF%9D%E5%A4%96%E5%B0%B1%E9%86%AB%E8%A2%AB%E6%8B%92%E6%94%B6-464587.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市林甸县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，在大庆市林甸个体种子商店任会计工作。因修炼法轮功，二十二年来曾多次遭中共警察抓捕、抄家、关押、被停发工资等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，由黑龙江省公安厅“督办”，大庆市公安局和林甸县公安局出动五十多个便衣警察，暴力抓捕了大庆市林甸县法轮功学员薛丽威、王玉红、路朝波、董娜、陈卫波等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，大庆让胡路区法院枉法判决：路朝波、王玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。薛丽威、陈卫波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款四万元，董娜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚款三万元。关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。王玉红刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王玉杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，长春市绿园区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住长春市绿园区青年路春天花园二十号楼。<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年，王玉杰开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午八点左右，王玉杰和另一法轮功学员街上宣传法轮功，被警察绑架到派出所，随后被抄家，家里的真相币、所有的钱、大法书籍、播放器等被抢走。王玉杰在派出所被关押十二个多小时后放回。警察对她说，回家等着法院判决吧。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又被警察抓捕，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现已上诉到中级法院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王玉玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省淄博市淄川区洪山镇解庄村老年法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月下旬，王玉玲先后两次在石湖和洪山大集讲真相时，被淄川区城南派出所便衣警察跟踪、抓捕到淄川公安分局，审讯至晚上十点左右，恐吓她家人交<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>元才放她回家。期间，王玉玲被强制按手印、抄家，抢劫走了所有大法书籍和资料，后被所谓“取保候审”、监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，王玉玲在家中被洪山镇派出所警察抓捕至派出所，两天后被关押至淄博市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，王玉玲被淄川区法院视频庭审，庭审中只播放了王玉玲在集市上讲真相被监控拍下的照片，未当庭宣判。现在得知王玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/28/450175.html#229272375-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/28/450175.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王玉梅：辽宁</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年出生，辽宁省鞍山市人。她淳朴厚道，与老伴<span lang="EN-US">1</span>起，来到居住在深圳市南山区的儿子家，帮忙带孙子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，王玉梅在深圳市赠送法轮功资料，被南山区公安分局警察抓捕，南山区公安分局对她行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，她在小区赠送邻里法轮功<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，遭遇中共洗脑毒害的民众的恶告。当天晚上十点左右，王玉梅在家中被南山公安分局国保和南头派出所警察再次抓捕，关押到南山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底，王玉梅被南山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。王玉梅认为此判决，提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，深圳市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446204.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446204.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">王月：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，河南省驻马店遂平县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，王月被遂平国保大队抓捕，关在驻马店看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">20212</span>月送河南新乡女监服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王云杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。王云杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王藏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，原名王玉文，笔名王藏、“小王子”，云南省楚雄市人，先锋诗人，自由作家，影视编剧，独立中文笔会会员，中国自由文化运动成员，中国曾押政治犯。王藏曾于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年底以“小王子”为笔名开始涉足网络诗歌习作，自此走上自由写作之路，并对极权文化予以批判。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，加入独立中文笔会，同年遭到官方威胁和长达<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个多月的监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年间因积极参与“中国自由文化运动”签名活动，又在《自由圣火》网站发文并设专栏、在博讯网上开设专栏发表文集等，而被贵州省遵义市警方于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月再次强制监视居住<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，荣获“<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>《自由圣火》写作奖”。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，正式启用笔名“王藏”，藉以表达“来生愿做藏人”的意愿。自<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起，因其积极参与多项维权民主活动、广交民主正义之士，并创作、推出了大量诗歌作品以及行为艺术，曾被北京当局多次警告威胁并驱离工作室和居住地，给其家庭造成诸多困扰。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因其在网上发布声援香港“雨伞革命”的打伞图片，随被北京市宋庄警方带走，其家被抄，之后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘于北京市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被北京市当局以同罪名正式逮捕，其罪由包括行为艺术和诗歌、文章，网上发布声援香港“占中”图片，声援郭飞雄，声援建三江被虐打人权律师，在网上祭奠林昭，关注藏人自焚事件，声援新疆维吾尔族学者伊力哈木•土赫提、法轮功问题、纪念“六四”及揭批文革等多项内容。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被取保候审释放；据悉，其在被审讯期间遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4.30</span>分左右，被云南省楚雄市公安机关突然以涉嫌煽动颠覆罪由带走，一直无任何消息。后王藏及夫人王利芹二人均被以“煽动颠覆国家政权”罪逮捕，王藏于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被正式逮捕，王利芹于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被正式逮捕，二人已经于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月中旬被移送云南省楚雄州检察院审查起诉。王藏被羁押在云南楚雄市看守所。指控王藏煽动颠覆国家政权罪名案件事实基本上就是他<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年那次被抓捕出来后所公开的言论、接受的采访、书写的诗歌文章、以及行为艺术。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，代理律师经与云南省楚雄州检察院电话核实，王藏（王玉文）、王丽芹夫妇煽动颠覆国家政权案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日起诉到楚雄州中级法院。代理律师认为此前楚雄看守所不当限制律师会见，已经严重违法。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，王藏（王玉文）、王利芹夫妇涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案遭延期审限，本案最后审限从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再延期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午，云南楚雄州中级法院开庭宣判王藏、王利芹夫妇构成煽动颠覆国家政权，分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。王藏、王利芹均当庭表示不服判决，提起上诉。王藏刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日获悉王藏已入云南省第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/4-26.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/4-26.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_86.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_76.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王展：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（网名：远古邪恶大象），为公义及乡土发声的公民、就职于芬兰<span lang="EN-US">Finnish Meteorological Institute</span>的环保学者，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日入境中国时被中共警察逮捕，并罗织以“颠覆国家政权”罪名，目前拘押于沈阳市第一看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王自成</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：北京市平谷法轮功学员。原是平谷区盘峰宾馆职工，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年底，因坚持修炼法轮功，被盘峰宾馆无理开除。王自成因坚持修炼法轮功，曾遭<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次判刑，累计遭受<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，王自成在北京市平谷区马坊镇一家工厂上班，在班上被平谷区公安分局峪口派出所警察抓捕的，警察认定他发放法轮功资料是违法的。后又遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索钱财<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王子明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省东营市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营市东营区胜利派出所、东三路派出所、明月派出所、文汇派出所警察同时出动，商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽等法轮功学员被秘密绑架。商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽被劫持到东营市看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营区法院对商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽庭审，并判处：王子明<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，商兆香<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；张爱丽<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元。四人上诉到东营市中级法院中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。王子明刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王志山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北香河县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，老家香河县渠口镇东梨园村，是一位乡村医生。王志山因坚持真善忍信仰，曾经被中共人员多次绑架到派出所、洗脑班迫害，遭酷刑折磨，诊所被迫停业，他流离失所十几年。张宪、王志山两位法轮功学员在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日见面时被香河县政保大队警察及派出所警察抓捕，被关押在香河县看守所，十月被批捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月两人被取保候审。后于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被香河县法院判刑，张宪被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王志山遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张宪、王志山被派出所警察又关押到香河县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/2_29.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，山西省太原市法轮功学员。太原市半坡西街居民，迎泽区人社局职工。王志燕因坚持法轮大法信仰，曾多次遭当地警察及社区人员抓捕、拘留、骚扰，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日遭鼓楼派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">212</span>日被太原市万柏林区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。王志燕上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被太原市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/30/%E5%B1%B1%E8%A5%BF%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%97%E7%87%95%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-440681.html"><b
