style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王忠胜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省抚顺市新宾县法轮功学员。曾在新宾县中共党校任教，高级讲师，三十多年的工龄，只因为修炼法轮功，坚持自己的信仰，被开除公职，多次被抓捕，关进劳教所和洗脑班迫害。为了维持生活，他曾经不得不靠走街串巷磨剪子菜刀艰难度日，后靠辅导学生谋生。二十多年来，他和妻子王桂兰饱尝了迫害给他们造成的所有经济损失、精神损失之苦，妻子王桂兰于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份离开人世。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被新宾县国保抓捕、抄家，后于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金四千元，曾被关押在抚顺南沟看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。王忠胜，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已七十五岁，现被关押在沈阳市东陵监狱三监区，他因被迫害严重，生命垂危，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月在监狱医院住院。据知情人透露：王忠胜被狱警逼坐小凳，不让活动，臀部溃烂，越来越严重。该知情者说，已无法治愈<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/7/447367.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/7/447367.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王忠实：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东淄博市博山区法轮功学员。王忠实<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日晚被抓捕，遭受冤狱十年，在山东省男子监狱十一监区历尽残酷折磨。出狱后，王忠实、高明洁于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被抓捕、构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑：王忠实获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，被勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；高明洁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万。二人上诉，被中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B7%84%E5%8D%9A%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%A0%E5%AE%9E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-431828.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B7%84%E5%8D%9A%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%A0%E5%AE%9E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-431828.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">旺堆（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，籍贯不详，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Wangdu</span>，拉萨大昭寺僧人，原澳大利亚伯<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>组织伯内特研究所（<span lang="EN-US">Burnet Institute</span>）雇员、拉萨市艾滋病毒预防工作者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日曾因参与和平示威而被捕，被当局判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并在拉萨市桑目叶监狱<span lang="EN-US">(Sangyip Prison)</span>服刑。服刑期间，又因参与了<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月抗议中共庆祝“解放”昌都<span lang="EN-US">40</span>周年纪念的活动，而被拉萨市中级法院加判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，随后被迁往拉萨市札基<span lang="EN-US">(Drachi)</span>监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，刑满释放，之后在澳大利亚一家<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>组织伯内特研究所任职，并在拉萨市及其邻近的乡镇从事艾滋病专项预防服务，并用汉藏双语印制出版多种相关病源常识及预防手册、海报与传单；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被拉萨市警方突然抓走刑拘，理由是涉嫌“接触并提供国外反政府势力信息”，后被正式逮捕；因是累犯，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被西藏自治区拉萨市中级法院以“间谍罪”判处无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身。目前疑似在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑，其被探视权等均被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">汪宝玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、小周女士、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，汪宝玉被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">汪福明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年不到<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，江西省赣州人，大约<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年大学毕业，后在南昌市工作两年左右。汪福明因修炼法轮大法与传播法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被南昌市高新区公安分局抓捕、抄家。后被南昌市公安局高新区分局刑事拘留。近日获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/56.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/56.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/10/%E5%8D%97%E6%98%8C%E9%9D%92%E5%B9%B4%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%B1%AA%E7%A6%8F%E6%98%8E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-466948.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/10/%E5%8D%97%E6%98%8C%E9%9D%92%E5%B9%B4%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%B1%AA%E7%A6%8F%E6%98%8E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-466948.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">汪信全：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1950</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年代生人，湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市咸安区居民，法轮功学员。因信仰、宣传法轮功而于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午在家中被咸宁市咸宁区警方以涉嫌邪教罪抓捕、刑拘，被关押在咸宁市咸安区拘留所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">魏彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省江油市太平镇新华村法轮功学员。魏彬（魏兵）在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年遭判刑十年，在德阳监狱入监队，遭受毒打、烈日暴晒、长时间罚站等各种迫害。他父亲魏朝海<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被恶警绑架，之后被判刑七年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年也被送劫持到德阳监狱迫害，魏朝海于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被德阳监狱迫害致死。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，魏彬再次被捕，关押期间遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日魏彬被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元。这次是他第二次遭重判，现已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/23/443964.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/23/443964.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">魏淑杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，哈尔滨市香坊区魏淑杰在香坊区旭升南街海富山水文园小区发法轮功资料时，被举报，被香坊分局建筑街派出所抓捕。后魏淑杰被所谓的“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，魏淑杰外出买菜回来，在楼道里被抓捕，她被关进哈尔滨第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午九点，黑龙江省哈尔滨市道外区法院在没有通知家属、律师的情况下，对法轮功学员魏淑杰女士进行视频开庭。魏淑杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。魏淑杰关押在黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/19/450936.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/19/450936.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">魏永汉</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代出生，广东省海丰县人，广东省海丰县乌坎村民代表。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月曾因所在广东省海丰县乌坎村民不满当局私自非法变卖村民土地，获利<span lang="EN-US">9</span>亿元且被村干部分摊，从而引发举世关注的乌坎事件，又因乌坎村民多次举行大规模维权游行示威，推行村民民主选举制度，并与警方几次爆发大型反抗冲突，遂遭广东当局的疯狂报复，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余人被抓、被通缉，其亦被广东当局定为“乌坎魏永汉、洪永忠等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人聚众扰乱社会秩序，非法集会、游行、示威，聚众扰乱交通秩序，妨害公务，故意传播虚假信息案”首要分子。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被网上通缉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被陆丰县警方拘捕，后转正式逮捕，并被指控与维权代表李楚卢以暴力方法阻碍国家机关工作人员依法执行职务，构成“妨害公务罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日其案件在广东省海丰县法院开庭受审，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被广东省海丰县法院一审以“非法集会、游行、示威罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“妨害公务罪”等多项罪名，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前被羁押于海丰县公安局看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">尉国申：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、尉国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。当时被抓捕的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员被构陷到遵化市法院。河北唐山市遵化法院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日对<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、尉国申、付瑞英、陆彩云开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日尉国申被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">危美甜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女<span lang="EN-US">, </span>广州市花都区法轮功学员 一九八六年三月出生，家住广州市花都区新华街，是<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年春开始修炼法轮功的。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年下半年，危美甜在花都区新华街附近张贴了几张法轮功不干胶，被监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，危美甜被广州市花都区公安分局国保和新华派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家，家里手机、电脑、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、法轮功书籍等私人物品被抄走。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，危美甜被花都区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年底，危美甜遭荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元。危美甜不服非法判决，提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。危美甜已经被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">危文元：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日出生，重庆市南岸区人，维权公民，公民记者。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾因所属房屋被政府强拆，一直未予公平公正的拆迁赔偿，遂被迫上访维权；期间，因多次投诉未果，且屡遭政府截访打压，随开始关注、投身于弱势群体的维权活动，同时认识到公民捍卫民主、自由、人权的重要性，故而成为重庆知名的公民记者，并积极帮助重庆访民进行维权报导和呼吁；曾因发布数百篇维权报导而遭遇当局的数十次威胁打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年 <span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，曾因六四敏感时期而被警方关押<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天，并多处受伤；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因与维权公民兼公民记者王晶、肖建芳等多人进京维权，并到世界互联网大会现场举牌呼吁“保障互联网自由，停止打压维权讯息传播”，而遭警方围堵截访，被遣返后又遭重庆警方非法施暴；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因《重庆日报》报业集团涉嫌虚假报导，而与数十名维权公民和访民到该报社门前谴责抗议；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因有访民电告在重庆报社有人跳楼，其前往围观，看见报社内外确有大量访民和警察存在，在调查暗访中，其被警方带走失联，后得知被重庆市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又被重庆市渝中区警方以同罪名正式逮捕判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，在被关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半后，获释出狱。此前被羁押于重庆市第一看守所。出狱后，继续从事维权事业。危文元女士长期关注和支持黄琦母亲浦文清女士，长期关注李怀庆案件，对包艳女士提供帮助和支持。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日又被当局抓捕，据称罪名是涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，刑拘满<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天仍未释放。可能已遭批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">文举平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川成都法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十九岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日文举平与法轮功学员袁学芬在小区贴真相不干胶时，被小区监控发现，后遭警察抓捕。据悉，警察从文举平电瓶车上搜走十部手机，从中调取自动电话软件的真相语音内容，并追查电话卡拨打了上万个真相电话，遂以此为由，对他进行司法迫害。四川省成都市龙泉驿区法院<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">问德怀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东临沂市郯城县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，家住临沂市郯城县大院子乡黄沟崖村。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，郯城县公安局归昌乡派出所抓捕了问德怀。后得知其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，已被转入山东省济南监狱，有望<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月回家。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445754.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445754.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">闻庆芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省迁安市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，迁安市住房和城乡建设局职工。一九九八年四月，闻庆芳修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，闻庆芳在外出办事途中，被迁安市公安局警察抓捕，被关押在唐山市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，迁安法院庭审闻庆芳。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被迁安市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/14/%E4%BF%A1%E4%BB%B0%E7%9C%9F%E5%96%84%E5%BF%8D%E6%9B%BE%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E9%97%BB%E5%BA%86%E8%8A%B3%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-464162.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/14/%E4%BF%A1%E4%BB%B0%E7%9C%9F%E5%96%84%E5%BF%8D%E6%9B%BE%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E9%97%BB%E5%BA%86%E8%8A%B3%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-464162.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武桂芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁。黑龙江巴彦县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，黑龙江巴彦县龙泉乡派出所警察将七十三岁的武桂芝叫去派出所，然后，将其绑架到巴彦县公安局，由女警察轮班看守。后武桂芝被告知自己被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武见男：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省籍人，基督徒，华西改革宗区会成员，四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会长老，中国在押良心犯。因笃信基督，并在四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会前长老郝鸣退休之后，由教会信众一致推举，被聘为该教会新任职的长老级神职人员，故而在教会里有极好的口碑，但也成为中共四川当局需要严打狠批的重要对象；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日， 成都秋雨圣约教会突遭成都警方的大抓捕，王怡牧师夫妇及秋雨圣约教会的诸多神职人员，如覃德富、李英强、李子虎等长老、牧者和同工（即教会神职服侍人员）百余人尽被成都警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>煽动颠覆国家政权罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>或<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑拘 ；后因打压扩大化，同年<span lang="EN-US">12 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>日，其所在四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会亦受冲击，教会会所被德阳市旌阳区警方与辖区城北街道办、小区等多方工作人员连手闯入，正在查经的信徒被驱离，教会正常的敬拜活动被 取缔，甚至提供教会租用房屋的房东也遭警方施压，被强行要求撕毁与教会签订的房屋租赁合同，让教会当天就得搬离会堂场所；因其与教会其他牧者、长老、同工与诸多信众拒绝了当局这一无理要求，表示仍将继续进入会堂敬拜，随其等神职人员之后频遭当局跟踪和监控，其教会也于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25 </span>日被四川省民政厅正式取缔<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其曾与退休后又在成都市秋雨圣约教会供职的郝鸣长老、贵阳市仁爱教会的张春雷长老（现已被贵州当局抓捕）等人公开同情、支援已被抓捕判刑的王怡牧师，并勇于、乐于说明成都秋雨圣约教会共度难关，随再遭当局更进一步强烈打压<span lang="EN-US">;</span>是日，其与其妻、郝鸣长老夫妇二人，以及教会的同工刘五一、刘永波、 蓝恩光等数人被四川省德阳市旌阳区警方统一抓走，两天之后，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其余人等都陆续被放，唯其及郝鸣长老被警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>诈骗罪<span lang="EN-US">" </span>转为正式刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24 </span>日，又被德阳市旌阳区检察院以同罪由正式批捕。目前被羁押于德阳市看守所（四川省德阳市双东镇龙凤村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">618017</span>）<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_80.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_80.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北律师武全<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日在新浪博客实名举报张家口市人大常委会副主任王志军。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，武全被张家口警方以涉嫌敲诈勒索罪刑事拘留。在对武全刑事拘留后，办案单位再向社会发出了线索征集的函件。此种先抓人再收集证据的知法犯法的行径在<span lang="EN-US">709</span>系列案中表现的淋漓尽致。这次又用在武全律师身上。令舆论哗然。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉其遭张家口市桥西区法院重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴长青</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：男，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九六一年一月出生；吴跃真，系吴长青女儿，一九八六年三月出生。吴长青、吴跃真父女家住广东揭阳市惠来县惠城镇。因使用法轮功基站发送信息，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被揭阳市国保和惠来县国保开三辆车围堵，抓捕后被关押到惠来县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，吴长青、吴跃真父女被惠来县法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，吴长青被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，吴跃真被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。父女俩上诉到揭阳市中级法院，均维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴成收：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潍坊市潍城区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月生，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年后，因坚持修炼法轮功，遭受长期迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点半左右，吴成收去上班时，被潍坊高新区公安局国保大队抓捕。关押在潍坊市看守所，后遭秘密审判，吴成收被判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元。二零二二年九月二十二日，被劫持到济南男子监狱遭受迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/1/450301.html#2293022452-3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴春雄：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月出生，广东省揭阳市揭西县人，揭阳市榕城区东升街道办事处新河村建阳路南<span lang="EN-US">3</span>区居民，揭阳市创致科技有限公司负责人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月起，曾因信仰法轮功而从网上购置打印机、纸册、切纸机和装订机等工具，在其经营的创致科技有限公司及居民住宅区私印法轮功宣传手册，同时，又利用微信组建法轮功群，发布许多相关法轮功信息和图片等，随很快引起广东省揭阳市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室”注意，并对其等数人进行严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，因其公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的宣传讯息，旋即被广东省揭阳市网员警觉，遂被揭阳市东升派出所警方从其所在公司抓走刑拘，其家及公司均遭查抄；另有其公司员工和友人唐建群、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人亦被当天抓走，并被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘；后被揭阳市榕城区检察院以“同案犯”、同罪名正式批捕，并被羁押于揭阳市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">1</span>行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案（另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被另案处理）被榕城区检察院正式起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案在广东省揭阳市榕城区法院统一受审；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法宣判；其中，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元；</b>另有唐建群、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华亦被分别判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月不等，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元—<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元不等；其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人不服判决，均向揭阳市中级法院提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，经广东省揭阳市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">吴春雄刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</b>目前在广东省四会监狱（广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘济广北路，广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴德修：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省蛟河市法轮功学员，系蛟河市松江乡永乡村农民，于一九九六年六月开始修炼法轮功。中共发动迫害法轮功后，他因坚守信仰、向民众讲清法轮功真相，而多次被中共人员抓捕，被关过洗脑班、看守所，并于三次被劳教，总计四年。在吉林市劳教所、吉林省九台劳教所、长春朝阳沟劳教所劳教期间，吴德修遭酷刑折磨，酷刑方式令人发指。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日吴德修被蛟河市民主派出所警察抓捕后，被当地公检法封锁信息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月家人才得知，中共公检法在不通知家属的情况下秘密开庭，吴德修已被舒兰市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被关押在公主岭监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457130.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457130.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴冬梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：吴冬梅</span>被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴方玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京延庆法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚，法轮功学员杨进香和丈夫韩仕民，以及郭金山、吴方玲等被抓捕。郭金山和韩仕民被关押在延庆看守所，杨进香和吴方玲被关押在昌平看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家人得知，北京延庆区吴方玲、杨进香、韩仕民、郭金山被判刑——吴方玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，杨进香<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，韩仕民<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，郭金山<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。吴方玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/13/447593.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/13/447593.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴风桃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九六四年一月出生，家住揭阳普宁市流沙镇白沙陇村。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，吴风桃被普宁市公安局和大南山派出所警察抓捕，关押到普宁市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，法院到普宁市看守所宣判，吴凤桃被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴刚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日出生，天津市和平区人，天津市某中学教师，抗强拆维权公民，中国在押维权人士。早期吴刚曾因其住宅被天津地方政府强拆，后其工作岗位又遭辞退，随被迫走上维权上访之路；近年来，曾因参与多起维权活动，尤其是参与声援天津北辰抗暴维权者王国廷案被当局枉法重判、维权公民在天津市人大门前举牌进行和平请愿等，而遭当局多次拘捕打压：<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日吴刚曾被天津警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被警方以涉嫌“扰乱单位秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，吴刚再次因参与维权抗争而被天津市和平区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被以同罪名转正式逮捕，关押在天津市南开区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，吴刚案件在天津市和平区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被天津市中级法院第两次庭审，终以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，吴刚刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因吴刚一直要求约见区人大代表，遂于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬突然失踪；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，知其被天津市河西区大营门派出所警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。目前被羁押于天津市河西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴海波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省湛江市霞山区法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月出生，大学毕业，原湛江市外加剂制药厂技术员，家住霞山区椹川大道中。一九九六年初修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七月中共江泽民团伙疯狂迫害法轮功后，因坚持修炼法轮功，吴海波屡遭中共迫害，曾入狱<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，他又被霞山区公安分局国保和新村派出所警察抓捕、构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚款五千元。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/2/458374.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/2/458374.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴孔大：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原是海南省定安县龙湖镇中心学校教师，多年来长期关注并转发民主宪政维权方面的信息，并多次对学校和政府提意见，遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底，吴老师因在微信群转发人权律师王全璋李和平被逼迁、何方美案等良心犯情况，被当地警方带到派出所，随后又被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日吴孔大被以被当地警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留，后遭批捕。目前羁押在海口第二看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/blog-post_11.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/blog-post_11.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span class="MsoHyperlink"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴玲娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴美芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东清远的失地农民维权代表。其所在的连州市丰阳镇其美村因为修高速公路需要征地，原村里负责人于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年趁村民外出做事，冒充村民在征地协议上签字，并侵吞集体土地征收补偿款。正在外面打工的其丈夫郭雪来接村民电话，立即回家和村民一起到镇政府讨说法，结果刚到镇政府大门口，十几村民就被抓捕了，其中郭雪来被以“扰乱国家工作机关秩序罪”判刑三年！后吴美芬为了替夫伸冤而被迫上访。郭雪来说：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份我爱人在北京信访时，给我们地方政府接访的人骗回来，说要保护我们的合法权益，解决我们的合理诉求，一个月后我收到逮捕通知书，说她“涉嫌扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”关押在铅山县看守所，就是这样得到党和政府的“保护”。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，郭雪来接到连州市法院电话，问要不要给他涉嫌“扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”的妻子吴美芬安排援助律师，郭雪来很清楚，所谓援助律师实际上就是官派律师，纯属为公检法“点炮”的，就断然拒绝了。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴启慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省绵阳市江油市法轮功学员。杜志俊、吴启慧夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被江油市公安局国保大队抄家，抢走电脑和所有大法书籍并被抓捕。杜志俊被抓捕到江油市看守所，吴启慧被抓捕到绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，杜志俊被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半；吴启慧被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴文章：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。吴文章刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴秀琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省白山市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，家住吉林省白山市靖宇县。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，吴秀琴多次被抓捕、关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱多次遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，靖宇县公安局国保大队大队长于学军，闯入吴秀琴租住的公寓，实施抓捕、抄家、抢劫，并把她关押到白山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日吴秀琴被白山市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%99%BD%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E5%90%B4%E7%A7%80%E7%90%B4%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434439.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴旭钦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日吴艳华与丈夫关兴涛被抓捕、构陷，后被大庆市让胡路区法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害。其丈夫关兴涛被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。吴艳华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1"><b minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴亚楠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，南开大学副教授，山东省高密市人，生于<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，山东大学政治学与公共管理学院本科、中国人民大学哲学院硕士、博士，因支持在乌鲁木齐大火后抗议的学生，先是被学校领导谈话，随后被要求删除网上言论，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬被强制带去做精神病检查，后一直音信全无，被强迫失踪至今。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_46.html<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p
